Description of the invention (12) The compound of formula (I) can also be used for the treatment of various filamentous mycetes such as Geotrichum clavatum, Mycelia ( Such as B. gerbilii), Blastoschizomyces (such as BlastozochimyCes capitatus), spore mycelia (such as S. sclerotiorum) Scedosporium (such as Scedosporium apiosperum), Cladosporium (such as Scavenger spores) Infections caused by bottle-shaped yeast. The compound of formula (I) can also be used to treat infections caused by protozoa such as Toxoplasma gondii, Cryptoperidum, Leishmania, Tripanosna, Giardia trichomoniasis. The in vitro evaluation of the anti-smear activity of the compounds of the present invention is performed on liquid or solid media using a two-fold serial dilution technique of anti-smear bacteria. This technique measures the inhibition of anti-smear agents at 37 ° C after 24 to 48 hours The minimum inhibitory concentration (MIC) of the growth of Candida. In practice, clinically relevant pathogens, such as Candida albicans, are cultivated with a series of agar plates or broth microdilution series containing a double dilution of antimycobacterial agent. Then measure the growth of the candida in the agar dish or broth microdilution series and record the appropriate MI C value. The MF C value (that is, the minimum concentration of anti-mycobacteria that kills at least 99.9% of pathogens in the original liquid medium) will be determined by subculture of 0.01 and 0.1 microliter broth in the control cavity without drug. Pathogens grow in the recesses, and other soil fat dish recesses grow without pathogens. The in vivo evaluation of the compound of formula (I) is based on a series of different dosimetry in which administration (eg, subcutaneous administration, oral administration, intraperitoneal administration or intravenous administration) is inoculated with Candida albicans strains. Untreated mice died within 3 to 9 days, and the dose that prevented 50% of infected mice from dying was recorded. -15- Use the Chinese National Standard Rate (CNS) 84 specifications (21〇x297mm) (please read the precautions on the back before filling out this page). 乂. 、 1T.    經濟部中央標準局員工消費合作社印製 由於式（i)化合物具抗眞菌活性，可用於治療人及動物的 各種眞菌感染。此類感染包括表面的，皮的，皮下的及系 統的霉菌感染，如呼吸道感染，胃腸道感染，心血管感染 ，尿道感染，中樞神經系統（CNS)感染，念珠菌病及慢性 枯液念珠菌病（如鵝口瘡及陰道念珠菌病）及由眞菌引起的 皮膚感染，皮及粘膜念珠菌病，包括癖及白癖感染在内的 膚眞菌病，香港腳，甲溝炎，花斑癬，紅癖，擦爛，眞菌 性泡瘆’念珠菌外陰炎及外耳炎。也可用作預防劑以預防 系統性及局部性眞菌感染。用作預防劑時，可作爲選擇性 腸去污染計劃的一部分以預防發生於免疫減弱病人的感染（ 例如愛滋病病人，接受化學治療的癌症病人，及器官移植 病人）。於某些疾病或醫原性情況下可能也需在抗生素治療 期預防眞菌的過度生長。 用於治療時’本發明化合物可以其原料藥給予，但較佳 是使用其醫藥調配物。是以本發明還提供醫藥調配物，含 有式（I)化合物及其醫藥上可接受的鹽，以及一或多種醫藥 上可接受的載劑，並且視需要含有其他治療及/或預防成 分。”可接受的” 一詞意爲與其他成分相容的並對接受者無 害的。 本發明組合物包括特別調配成用於經口給予、經頰給予 、注射給予、植入給予、直腸給予、局部給予、經眼或泌 尿生殖系統給予的形式的組合物，或適於吸入或吹入給予 形式的組合物。 供經口給予的錠或膠囊可含傳統的賦形劑，如結合劑， ________；_ -16- 本紙張尺度適用中國國家標準（CNS ) A4規格（210X297公釐） ' (請先閱讀背面之注意事項再填寫本頁) •'户. 、11 經濟部中央標準局員工消費合作社印裝 Printed by the Employee Consumer Cooperative of the Central Bureau of Standards of the Ministry of Economic Affairs. The compound of formula (i) has antimycobacterial activity and can be used to treat various infections of human mycetes. Such infections include surface, skin, subcutaneous, and systemic fungal infections, such as respiratory infections, gastrointestinal infections, cardiovascular infections, urinary tract infections, central nervous system (CNS) infections, candidiasis, and candidal candidiasis Diseases (such as thrush and vaginal candidiasis) and skin infections caused by candidiasis, candidiasis of the skin and mucous membranes, skin candidiasis including addiction and white addiction infections, Hong Kong foot, paronychia, variegation Ringworm, red addiction, abrasion, mycobacterial alveolar'candidiasis vulvitis and otitis externa. It can also be used as a preventive agent to prevent systemic and local infections. When used as a preventative, it can be used as part of a selective bowel decontamination program to prevent infections that occur in immunocompromised patients (eg, AIDS patients, cancer patients undergoing chemotherapy, and organ transplant patients). In some diseases or iatrogenic conditions, it may be necessary to prevent the overgrowth of mycetes during antibiotic treatment. When used for treatment, the compound of the present invention can be administered as its raw material, but it is preferred to use its pharmaceutical formulation. Therefore, the present invention also provides pharmaceutical formulations containing the compound of formula (I) and pharmaceutically acceptable salts thereof, and one or more pharmaceutically acceptable carriers, and optionally containing other therapeutic and / or prophylactic ingredients. The term "acceptable" means compatible with other ingredients and not harmful to the recipient. Description of invention (36), prepared by Wen ’. Pharmaceutically acceptable salts can also be prepared from other salts, including other pharmaceutically acceptable salts of compounds of formula (1), using conventional methods. Metabolically unstable esters of compounds of formula (I) can be prepared by reaction with the existing bases by conventional methods. Similarly, metabolically unstable esters can also be formed with free radicals present on the molecule. The novel compound of formula (XII) can be prepared according to the fermentation method described later, or can be prepared by demethylation of sodarin by a biotransformation method. The fermentation method involves culturing a microorganism capable of producing the compound of formula (XII), and then separating the compound of formula (XII) from the culture. The microorganism capable of producing the compound of formula (XII) may be a variant of D. arachnoides. This strain can be confirmed by analyzing the survival rate of the mutant by screening test samples obtained by fermentation of microorganisms by standard methods. In particular, the microorganisms that are convenient to use are the strains of arachnid coccidioides stored in the constant culture collection of CAB International Mycological Institute, Genetic Resource Reference Collection Bakeham Lane, Egham, Surrey TW20 9TY, United Kingdom. This strain was received by this organization on June 10, 1994, and the acquisition number was given as IMI 362184, and the date of receipt and the date of confirmation of survival were indicated on June 13, 1994 and 21, respectively. This institution is accepted as an international depository (Internati〇nai Depository) authority under the Buda Pace Treaty. For the characteristics proven so far by IMI 362 184, see Example 74. In yet another aspect, the present invention provides the original IMI 362184 microorganism and variants thereof. These methods include ionizing radiation, chemical methods such as N-methyl-N'-nitro-N-nitroisomai (n TG), thermal 'gene technology' such as gene recombination and gene conversion, treatment, and Selective natural variant technology. The preparation of the compound of formula (XII) by fermentation can be accomplished by traditional methods, that is, cultivating suitable microorganisms in the presence of assimilable sources of carbon, nitrogen, and mineral salts, and then isolating the desired product. The sources of assimilable carbon, nitrogen, and mineral salts can be supplied by simple or compound nutrients. Carbon sources generally include glucose, maltose, starch, glycerin, molasses dextrin, lactose, sucrose, fruit sugar, galactose, inositol, D_mannose 'soybean oil' carboxylic acid, amino acid 'glyceride, alcohol , Alkanes and vegetable oils. The carbon source generally constitutes 0.5 to 10% by weight of the fermentation base. Fruit sugar 'glucose and sucrose represent preferred carbon sources. Nitrogen sources generally include soybean meal, corn broth, lees, yeast extract, cottonseed meal, glands, ground hard fruit powder, malt extract, molasses, casein 'amino acid mixture, ammonia (gas or solution ), Ammonium or nitrate, urea and other amides can also be used. Nitrogen sources generally constitute 0.01 to 10% by weight of the fermentation base. The nutrient mineral salts that can be used in the culture medium include commonly used sodium, sodium, aluminum, iron, iron, zinc, aluminum, aluminum, phosphate, sulfate, Salts of vapors and carbonate ions. -40- This paper scale is applicable to China ’s B Family Standard (CNS) A4 specification (210X297 public daughter (please read the precautions on the back and then fill out this page) Λ. Description of the invention (38) One *-The cultivation of microorganisms is generally at 20. To 40 ° C, preferably 2 〇. (: To 35C 'especially about 25. (:, sometimes need to be carried out under ventilation and shaking (such as shaking or stirring). At the beginning of the medium can be inoculated with a small amount of mycelium and / or spores obtained The plant-based inoculum can be transferred to the fermentation substrate, or to one or more seed stages, where it is further grown, and then transferred to the main fermentation substrate. The fermentation is generally carried out at pH 3.5 to 9.5, preferably 4.5 to 7.5. It may be necessary to add alkali or acid to the fermentation substrate to maintain the pH in the desired range. Suitable alkalis that can be added include alkali metal hydroxides, such as aqueous sodium hydroxide or potassium hydroxide. Suitable acids include Mineral acids, such as hydrochloric acid, sulfuric acid or succinic acid .. Fermentation can be carried out 4-30 , Preferably about 5-15 days. To control excessive foaming, anti-foaming agent can be added, the time of addition depends on the need. Carbon and / or nitrogen source can also be added to the fermentation matrix as needed. Compound of formula (XII) Mainly attached to cells, it can be added with acid or water-soluble organic solvent, more preferably with alkali (such as sodium hydroxide) to make a solution. The cells in the solution can be separated by centrifugation, traditional filtration method or membrane filtration This liquid can be re-used with acid, such as sulfuric acid, if necessary, and treated to a pH of less than 6 (eg, about 4.5). The compound of formula (XII) can be separated and purified by various distribution techniques, such as washing away by adsorption, Shen Dian, classification: Crystallization, solvent extraction, and liquid-liquid distribution methods can also be used in combination. Separation and purification of the compound of formula (IX) is most suitable for adsorption on a solid support followed by washing away. Suitable solid supports include dioxide ; Non-functional large-mesh adsorption resins, such as cross-linked styrene divinylbenzene polymer resins, such as CG161 and Amberlite XAD-2, XAD-4, XAD-16 or XAD-1180 -41 -i China National Standard (CNS) A4 specification (210X297 PCT) ~ --------- f Λ ------ IT ------ f (Please read the Notes on the back to fill out this page)

The compound of formula (XII) can also be separated and purified using a liquid anion exchanger such as LA2. A suitable solvent for washing away the compound of formula (XII) will naturally depend on the nature of the adsorption. When using polymer resins (such as X AD-16), solvents that are compatible with water, such as methanol, acetone, isopropanol, or acetonitrile, can be used in different proportions with water. During the extraction / separation process, the presence of the compound of formula (χπ) can be detected by using the optical rotation property or other properties of the secondary compound by traditional techniques, such as high performance liquid chromatography (HPLC) or UV spectroscopy.    International Mycological Institute, Genetic Resource Reference Collection Bakeham Lane, Egham, Surrey TW20 9TY。此菌株係於1994年8月11日由此機構收到，給予的 取得編號爲IMI 362947，存活證實曰期分別爲1994年8月 19日。此機構依布達佩斯條約被承認爲國際存儲 (International Depository)權威。就IMI 362947到目前爲止 所證實的特性見實例26所述。 本發明進一步提供微生物IMI 362947本身及其突變種。 取得IMI 362947變種及其基因物質的方法與前述操作IMI 362184之方法相似。 索達里新也可使用生物轉化法由索達林製備。生物轉化 的完成是：將索達林於含有合適的微生物及碳源與氮源（包 括前述的各種碳源與氮源）的培養物内培育，然後從培養物 内分離索達里新。 能使索達林轉化成索達里新的微生物可用小尺度試驗並 用標準方法分析取得的試驗樣品（如用HPLC分析）確定。發 明人等已證實一種此種微生物，並已存入National Collections of Industrial and Marine Bacteria Limited (NCIMB), 23 St. Machar Drive, Aberdeen AB2 1RY, International Mycological Institute, Genetic Resource Reference Collection Bakeham Lane, Egham, Surrey TW20 9TY. This strain was received by this institution on August 11, 1994, and the obtained accession number was IMI 362947, and the date of survival confirmation was August 19, 1994, respectively. This institution is recognized as an international depository authority under the Budapest Treaty. See Example 26 for the characteristics demonstrated so far by IMI 362947. The present invention further provides the microorganism IMI 362947 itself and its mutants. The method for obtaining the IMI 362947 variant and its genetic material is similar to the method for operating IMI 362184 described above. Sodarin can also be prepared from Sodarin using biotransformation. The biotransformation is accomplished by growing Sodarin in a culture containing suitable microorganisms and carbon and nitrogen sources (including the aforementioned various carbon and nitrogen sources), and then separating Sodarin from the culture. New microorganisms that can convert Sodarin into Sodarin can be determined by small-scale tests and analysis of test samples obtained by standard methods (such as HPLC analysis). The inventors have confirmed one such microorganism and have deposited it in National Collections of Industrial and Marine Bacteria Limited (NCIMB), 23 St. Machar Drive, Aberdeen AB2 1RY, 
 
 
   Scotland。NCIMB於1994年8月4日收到此菌株，於同一天 接受此菌株作專利並證實此微生物爲活的。此微生物爲棒 狀菌種（Coryneform species)，其特徵如實例2 7所述，已被 指定爲NCIMB 40675號。MCIMB爲布達佩斯條約所承認的 International Depository 權威。 -45- 本紙張尺度逋用中國國家橾準（CNS ) A4规格（210X297公釐） (請先閱讀背面之注意事項再填寫本頁) %Λ· Scotland. Description of the invention (43) The NCIMB 40675 microorganism and its variants are also provided on the other hand of the present invention. According to another aspect of the present invention, the inventors provided the genetic material of NCIMB 40675 and its variants, which can convert sodarin to sodaris. The method for obtaining the NCIMB 40675 variant and its genes is similar to the method for operating IMI 362184 described above. NCIMB 40675 can be cultivated on 20. To 40. (:, Preferably 20. to 35 C, most preferably about 28 ° C. Sometimes it needs to be carried out under ventilation and shaking (such as shaking or stirring). A small amount of mycelium and / Or spores. The resulting plant inoculum can be transferred to the fermentation substrate, or transferred to one or more seed stages (seed stages), where it is further grown (for example, about 3 days), and then transferred to the main fermentation Substrate. The main fermentation substrate may also contain sodarin, and the fermentation is generally carried out at a pH of 3.5 to 9.5, preferably 4.5 to 75. It may be necessary to add alkali or acid to the fermentation substrate to maintain the pH in the desired range. Suitable bases to be added include alkali metal hydroxides, such as aqueous sodium hydroxide or potassium hydroxide. Suitable acids include mineral acids such as hydrochloric acid, sulfuric acid or phosphoric acid. Fermentation can take 4-8 days, preferably about 6 days . To control excessive foaming, anti-foaming agents can be added, the time of addition depends on the need. Carbon and / or nitrogen sources can also be added to the fermentation substrate as needed. ”It should be understood that biotransformation can be accomplished according to various methods. Cells can be added to sodarin in eg buffers, used The solution in the fermentation substrate and water is inoculated and harvested. In addition, it is also feasible to isolate and use the appropriate enzyme (while using the appropriate coenzyme) or to clone and overexpress the enzyme. Sodarin is separated from the fermentation broth It can be done by the general method mentioned above. (Please read the precautions on the back before filling this page), 11

Distilled water was added to maintain the culture volume at 500 liters. Add PPG2000 anti-foaming agent as needed to control foaming. Reverse phase HPLC was used to identify Sodarin in all broth extracts (+ 1% trifluoroacetic acid in acetonitrile in water). After n days', the culture was harvested when the broth extract sample showed a sodarin titer of 0.6 g / liter. Make the fermentation broth contain 0.1M sodium hydroxide, store it at ambient temperature overnight and filter with Dicalite on the rotary hollow filter (add 10/0 Dicalite as a filter aid in the broth). The filtrate was adjusted to 6-7 with concentrated sulfuric acid to 6-7, and this solution was added to XAD16 resin (10 times the volume of the filtrate / resin). Wash the adsorbent with water and acetone / water (1: 3) to get a clear effluent, and then _ wash away the sodarin with acetone: water (3: 1; charge two column volume). The flow rate for this process is 1-2 column volumes / hour. Concentrate the eluate to a small volume (85 liters). The pH of the concentrate was adjusted to 3 with squamous acid, and the sodarin precipitated out by standing at ambient temperature overnight. Pour out the floating solution, then centrifuge to discard the floating solution. Dissolve the centrifugal pills and the precipitate in 75% acetonitrile aqueous solution to obtain 3.9 liters of dark standard solution. To this solution was added 1.0 liter of 0.2M NH4Η2Ρ04 'under stirring, and then the pH of the solution was adjusted to 4.0 with squamous acid, and the final volume was 5.0 liter with nearly 60% acetonitrile_〇im NH4H2P〇4. The above crude Sodarin solution (5_0 liter) was subjected to preparative HPLC treatment with 10 injections (450-550 ml each time) on a 7 mm Kromasil C8 column (15 cm X 25 cm) with a mobile phase of 50% Acetonitrile-0.1 \ 1> 1114112? 〇4, ie 114 (add 50 liters of water to 100 liters of acetone 'containing 575 grams of NH4H2P〇4 and 40 milliliters of h3P〇4), with a flow rate of 600 milliliters / minute, with UV absorbance Nano) determination. Collect eluent in portions between 15.4 and 19.2 minutes. Concentrate 10 injections of eluent (2 3 liters), dilute with water to 50 liters, and then use this solution at 28-49-paper size to use the Chinese National Standard (CNS) A4 specifications (210X297 %) ---- --------- 'X II 〆 (please read the precautions on the back before filling in this page), 11 A7 38l644 ._____ B7 V. Description of the invention (47) Liter / hour speed Haw back through the Kromasil column. The column was washed with water (25 liters) and then washed away with 90% acetonitrile (10 liters). The eluate was evaporated to 300 ml of residue, and then dried to prepare the title compound as a beige powder (105.6 g). The product was analyzed by mass spectrometry (MS) and nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) and showed the same as the confirmed sodarin sample. Description of the invention (52) 'The exudate is a clear solution. After adjusting the pH to 5.2 with concentrated sulfuric acid, the exudate was loaded on a XAD16 resin column at a loading rate of 2 column volumes / hour, and finally 32 grams of 4, -demethyl sodarin was loaded per liter of resin. This column was washed with 0.1% volume / volume phosphoric acid, and then with 20% volume / volume acetonitrile / water (each with 10 column volumes) at a rate of 2 column volumes / hour. The column was washed off with 65% acetonitrile / water, and the washing off rate was 2 column volumes / hour. Discard the 0.75 column volume that flowed out first, and collect 85% of the loaded 4. · demethylsodarin from the eluate of 1.6 column volume later. This large amount of washed material was treated with 20% weight / volume DE52 cellulose with stirring for 5 minutes, and then taken out and filtered. An aliquot of the eluate treated with DE52 was concentrated using a rotary evaporator to 62% of the original volume (43% acetonitrile). The concentrated eluate was kept at 4 for 15 hours to crystallize, and the collected solid was filtered with a glass porous filter. The crystals were washed with 30% volume / volume acetonitrile / water of 4 cake volume and dried at 30 ° C. The title compound (94 g) collected from the concentrated eluate was a light gray solid. The eluate was evaporated to dryness at room temperature, and the residue was dissolved in a 50% volume / volume solution of acetonitrile in water (9 ml). Description of the invention (98) ~ Yu Bingwang: add tetroxide to the ice-cold mixture in water (8: 1 ′ 9 ml) (2/5% by weight solution in 2-methyl-2-propanol, 0.075 ml). Description of the invention (144) The intermediate 89b (250 mg) and imidazole (catalytic amount) were dissolved in anhydrous tetrahydrofuran under argon. Sodium hydride (45 mg) was added, and the suspension was stirred at room temperature for 20 minutes. Add carbon disulfide (14μl), continue stirring for 20 minutes, and add methyl iodide (150μl). After 2 hours, ethyl acetate (10 mL) was added to stop the reaction. Then water (5 mL) was added dropwise. This mixture was separated between ethyl acetate (50 mL) and water (50 mL), and the organic layer was washed with water and brine, then dried and evaporated. The residue was analyzed and purified by flash chromatography on silica gel, and washed away with hexane: ethyl acetate (10: 1) to (8: 1) to obtain the title compound (211 mg). Example 7 5 Features of IMI 362947 IMI 362947 is a variant of D. arachnidus (ATCC 36386, NRRL 3 196), the ascospores of this strain are N-methyl-N, -nitro-N-nitrosoguanidine mutagenized It is separated afterwards. This strain differs from NRRL 3196 in that it produces more sodaline than NRRL 3 196 under the same conditions. Example 7 6 NCIMB 40675 銿 擞 NCIMB 40675 is aerobic 'Gram-positive, immobile irregular rods' in 28 ° C in 2% (weight / volume) yeast trypsin soybean At 48 hours of agar, lemon yellow, translucent, round, complete, raised, 0.5 mm in diameter colonies were produced. This microorganism grows well up to 37C, but it does not grow better than this strain at 45 ° C. There are no metachromatic particles, but it is catalase-positive, oxidative, and cannot metabolize glucose by fermentation. This strain can use the following carbon sources: _D_glucose, D_fruit sugar, p-hydroxyphenylacetic acid, D_mannose, methyl \ pyruvate, lactamide, D-trehalose and sucrose . This microorganism can only use a little D-gluconate, pyruvate, and salicin as the main carbon source. The colony and microscope morphology are similar to Corynebacterium ^ The difference with Corynebacterium is that the peptidoglycan of NCIMB 40675 contains ornithine instead of 2,6 · diaminopimelic acid or -216- This paper size is applicable Chinese National Standard (CNS) A4 ^ grid (2I0X297mm) (Please read the precautions on the back before filling in this page), -β 321644 A7 B7 V. Description of the invention (214) The racemic difference of monoaminobutyric acid Structure. Moreover, this microbial-containing complex mixture of fat and acid is also different from that contained in coryneform bacteria, namely 12-methyltetradecanoic acid, 14-methylhexadecanoic acid and 14-methylpentadecanoic acid. No alpha-branched-A-hydroxylated fatty acids were also detected. Based on these results, ncimb 40675 is closest to the following species of Actinomyces: Aureobacillus, Curtobacterium, or Cellulomonas. To clarify the taxonomic position of NCIMB 40675, the 1100 base pair portion of the 16S rRNA gene is compared with 24 other species representing Actinobacteria and related genera. The results of this analysis show that NCIMB 40675 is more closely related to the genus Staphylococcus aureus and Curtobacterium, but farther away from the genus Cellulomonas and the genus Corynebacterium. For more accurate confirmation of this strain, in addition to more chemical taxonomy and physiology tests, phylogenetic analysis can be performed to compare the rRNA genes of various regions of Chrysanthemum aureus and Curtobacterium.
